msg:The hotel environment is elegant, the architectural design is unique, and the location is a small island in the Garden Expo Park next to the Second Ring Road. The facilities are complete and the hygiene is very good. The service staff, whether the front desk or the lobby manager, are really considerate and thoughtful. We brought our parents, who are 80 years old. All the large piles of luggage were sent to the room by the hotel front desk girl and a man in charge of the lobby with two luggage carts and taken to the corresponding position. The room is beautiful and practical, and the balcony has a pleasant view. All the service staff greeted us with a smile, asked about our well-being, and took the initiative to prepare buckwheat pillows for the elderly. The elderly said it was so considerate and comfortable. I just came to Yulin for the first time and passed by Guilin overnight. I didn't expect such a small city to have such a good hotel! And the pleasant price of more than 400 yuan made me feel happy at the first stop of my trip. In the evening, there were fruits and red bean and barley soup in the room, which was delicious and nutritious. The buffet breakfast on the second day was comprehensive and thoughtful, tasted good, and had a full range of varieties. My parents were very happy and said that the girls of the hotel service staff were so gentle and beautiful, which was pleasing to the eye!
